Dear interest of exceptional designer wall clocks

Please find in the attachment your requested catalog and the price list

of ChronArte Quadro clocks.

The clocks are radio controlled (DCF 77). In european countries with

time deviation from Central Europe Time(GB, Portugal, eastern Europe) we

have a special solutions to show the exact local time.

For outside Europe there is a quartz version available.

In case of any questions don't hesitate to contact us.

The ChronArte Team
